  Uses Pyodide to run code, detects and installs dependencies, and captures all outputs - perfect for agent-driven data analysis.
  
  Works with Pydantic AI and MCP clients.

### #mycosoft-platform (9 entries)

#### 💡 Notes & Ideas

- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet**: ---
  
  ## 6. Supabase Notes (Critical)
  
  - Postgres **must not** be exposed to WAN
  - Prefer:
    - Docker-internal networking
    - Access via VPN or SSH tunnel only
  - Only expose Supabase services that clients explicitly need
  - Treat Supabase as a private backend, not a public DB
  
  ---
  
  ## 7. Firewall Rules (Summary)
  
  ### Production (.201)
  Allow:
  - WAN → 80, 443
  - LAN/VPN → SSH, admin ports
  Block:
  - Everything else
  
  ### Sandbox / Test (.202 / .203)
  Allow:
  - LAN/VPN → reverse proxy ports
  - LAN/VPN → SSH
  Block:
  - All WAN inbound traffic
  
  ---
  
  ## 8. Port Philosophy (Why This Works)
  
  - Environment separation is **network-enforced**
  - Port numbers remain predictable
  - Docker configs stay clean (standard ports internally)
  - DNS-based routing scales without rework
  - Accidentally deploying prod to sandbox becomes obvious
  
  ---
  
  ## 9. Optional Enhancements
  
  - WireGuard or Tailscale for admin access
  - Bastion host (.

- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet**: ---
  
  ## 3. Host-Level Listening Ports
  
  ### Production (.201)
  
  | Port | Scope | Purpose |
  |-----|------|---------|
  | 80  | WAN  | HTTP → HTTPS redirect |
  | 443 | WAN  | HTTPS (reverse proxy) |
  | 8443 | LAN/VPN (optional) | Admin / debug HTTPS |
  | 22  | LAN/VPN only | SSH |
  
  ---
  
  ### Sandbox (.202)
  
  | Port | Scope | Purpose |
  |-----|------|---------|
  | 8080 | LAN/VPN only | HTTP (reverse proxy) |
  | 8443 | LAN/VPN only | HTTPS (reverse proxy) |
  | 22   | LAN/VPN only | SSH |
  
  `80/443` **closed** on sandbox to prevent mistakes.
  
  ---
  
  ### Test (.203)
  
  | Port | Scope | Purpose |
  |-----|------|---------|
  | 8081 | LAN/VPN only | HTTP (reverse proxy) |
  | 8444 | LAN/VPN only | HTTPS (reverse proxy) |
  | 22   | LAN/VPN only | SSH |
  
  ---
  
  ## 4. Internal Application Ports (Docker-only)
  
  These **should NOT** be published to the host unless there is a specific reason.
  
  | Service | Environment | Internal Port |
  |-------|

- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet**: # Myca VM Network & Port Scheme
  
  - Production
  - Sandbox
  - Test
  
  The goals are:
  - Predictability
  - Minimal accidental exposure
  - Clear separation of environments
  - Easy mental mapping at 02:00 during incident response
  
  ---
  
  ## 1. VM Inventory
  
  | Environment | Hostname (example)        | Static IP     |
  |------------|---------------------------|---------------|
  | Production | myca-prod                 | x.x.x.201     |
  | Sandbox    | myca-sandbox              | x.x.x.202     |
  | Test       | myca-test                 | x.x.x.203     |
  | (Optional) Shared / Observability | myca-ops | x.x.x.204 |
  | (Optional) Bastion / VPN | myca-bastion | x.x.x.205 |
  
  All VMs run:
  - Docker
  - Supabase
  - Reverse proxy (Traefik / NPM / Caddy)
  - Linux firewall (UFW / nftables / iptables)
  
  ---
  
  ## 2. Exposure Model (Important)
  
  Port numbers are **not security controls**.
  Network reachability + firewall rules + auth are the real controls.
  


- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet**: Agent deploy-  ensure that static IP’s are set on machines and noted in UI as static IP’s or they probably wont be shown in UI dashboard

- `2026-01-18` **nodefather**: These are some Deployment Lessons I learned as I am moving towards a more automated CI/CD Pipeline (Continuous Integration/Continuous Deployment or Delivery), which I will be implementing so all of us can modify or send to devs to modify in a clean fast way.  Also a current audit of VM which is now already changing for the better.
  
  CI/CD (Continuous Integration/Continuous Deployment or Delivery represents a set of operating principles and practices that enable software development teams to deliver code changes more frequently, reliably, and efficiently. It is a cornerstone of modern DevOps, automating the steps between developing code and deploying it to production. )

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather**: 3. Core Apps – "Google Apps, but for Mycology"
  
  These function like Google Docs, Sheets, and Drive, but for fungi research, simulations, and biological computing.
  
  Essential Apps:
  
  🔬 Petri Dish Simulator – A virtual growth environment for modeling mycelium interactions
  🍄 Mushroom Simulator – Simulates mushroom growth, genetic variables, and environmental impact
  🧪 Compound Simulator – Predicts fungal compound interactions, beneficial properties, and applications
  🌐 Spore Tracker – Tracks global spore movements and environmental interactions
  🗺 Fungi Map – Community-driven global mapping of fungi populations
  📜 Fungal Ancestry Database – Explore and contribute to the evolutionary history of fungi
  🤖 Myca AI Research Assistant – AI-driven assistant that overlays all apps
  
  🔧 Future Apps & Expansions:

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather**: Monetization & Business Model
  
  To sustain and grow Mycosoft’s platform while providing free access to core tools, the business model will be tiered access, device sales, and data licensing.
  
  ✅ Free Access:
  
  Basic search, NatureOS dashboard, Myca AI, and core apps are free for general users.
  
  
  ✅ Paid Tiers & Revenue Streams:
  
  Hardware Sales – Mushroom 1, SporeBase, Petraeus, and lab tools
  
  Premium Research Subscriptions – Advanced analytics, biobank access, and data storage
  
  Enterprise Solutions – B2B licensing for biotech, agriculture, and environmental industries
  
  Cloud Processing & API Access – Paid access for large-scale research projects
  
  
  ✅ Decentralized Science Funding:
  
  MycoDAO-powered research grants, crowdfunding, and community-backed science initiatives

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather**: Mycosoft.com Core Product Plan
  
  Goal: Make Mycosoft.com the central hub for fungal intelligence, data, research, and tools—structured like Google’s ecosystem, with a search-first interface, cloud applications, hardware integration, and AI-assisted interaction.
  
  
  ---
  
  1. Homepage – "The Google for Fungi"
  
  Purpose: A powerful, search-driven entry point into Mycosoft’s ecosystem.
  
  Core Features:
  
  ✅ Fungal Search Engine – A search bar that connects to MINDEX, Mycorrhizae Protocol, and open datasets like MycoBank, NCBI, and iNaturalist.
  ✅ Quick Links & Shortcuts – One-click access to key areas:
  
  🌱 Buy Devices – Purchase Mushroom 1, SporeBase, TruffleBot, Petraeus
  
  🔬 Submit Tissue – Send samples to the biobank for research & sequencing
  
  🧫 Request Tissue – Order specific mycelium or spores from the biobank
  
  🌎 Interact with Nature – Engage with simulations, databases, and live data feeds
  
  🤖 Talk to Myca – AI-powered mycology assistant and researc

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather**: 2. NatureOS – The "Cloud Dashboard"
  
  Purpose: The heart of Mycosoft’s ecosystem—similar to Google Drive, this is where all apps, data, and devices integrate into a personalized research & nature interface.
  
  Key Components:
  
  ✅ Dashboard with Modules:
  
  📊 Live Data from Devices – Connects to personal or public Mushroom 1 & SporeBase sensors
  
  🌿 Mycology Cloud Apps – Quick access to Petri Dish Simulator, Mushroom Simulator, Compound Simulator, Ancestry Database, Spore Tracker, Map, and Identification
  
  🔗 Fungal Database API – Connect to MINDEX and submit or retrieve fungal data
  
  🛠 Device Management – Users can control Mushroom 1, SporeBase, Petraeus from their dashboard
  
  💾 Fungal Biobank Access – Request, upload, and analyze tissue samples
  
  
  ✅ User Accounts & Cloud Storage:
  
  🔐 Personal Research Vault – Save and access previous simulations, DNA data, environmental monitoring logs
  
  📂 Community Contributions – Share datasets, findings, and reports
 

- `2024-10-07` **nodefather**: The AI-Scientist from SakanaAI is an open-source project designed for automating the scientific process through AI models. It leverages techniques like Bayesian optimization, reinforcement learning, and evolutionary algorithms to generate hypotheses, design experiments, and analyze data autonomously. 
  
  For Mycosoft, this tool could be integrated into NatureOS for automating fungal research. For example, it could help optimize mushroom growth conditions, manage large datasets from MushroomOne or SporeBase, or automate scientific discoveries related to mycelium signal processing. The backend can be enhanced to work with the Mycorrhizae Protocol for real-time scientific insights.

- `2024-11-15` **nodefather**: One of the first microprocessors.
  
  The Intel 4004 was developed and laid out by hand, using conventional schematics and some (at the time) quite unconventional fabricating techniques.
  
  It only had 2,600 transistors (well, I say “only,” but compared to modern CPUs with tens of billions of transistors that’s not a lot), and designing a circuit with 2,600 transistors is challenging but reasonable to do by hand.
  
  Here’s the schematic:

- `2024-10-06` **nodefather**: Mycosoft is pioneering earth-monitoring and biological data solutions through its NatureOS platform, leveraging field devices like Mushroom One and SporeBase for continuous environmental sensing. By utilizing soil and mycelium sensors, we offer a scalable, credible system for monitoring organic carbon in the soil, similar to MRV (Monitoring, Reporting, Verification) practices in regenerative agriculture. This enables real-time insights into soil health, carbon capture, and biodiversity restoration. Mycosoft envisions supporting global agriculture by integrating mycelium-driven carbon solutions and enhancing biodiversity through its robust data ecosystems.
  
  Our Impact:
  
  Global Ecosystem Support: Our tools aid farmers in fostering biodiversity and carbon sequestration.
  
  Sustainable Market Growth: By integrating our technologies, we aim to enhance soil health across ecosystems, ensuring sustainable agricultural practices.

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather**: 2. NatureOS – The "Cloud Dashboard"
  
  Purpose: The heart of Mycosoft’s ecosystem—similar to Google Drive, this is where all apps, data, and devices integrate into a personalized research & nature interface.
  
  Key Components:
  
  ✅ Dashboard with Modules:
  
  📊 Live Data from Devices – Connects to personal or public Mushroom 1 & SporeBase sensors
  
  🌿 Mycology Cloud Apps – Quick access to Petri Dish Simulator, Mushroom Simulator, Compound Simulator, Ancestry Database, Spore Tracker, Map, and Identification
  
  🔗 Fungal Database API – Connect to MINDEX and submit or retrieve fungal data
  
  🛠 Device Management – Users can control Mushroom 1, SporeBase, Petraeus from their dashboard
  
  💾 Fungal Biobank Access – Request, upload, and analyze tissue samples
  
  
  ✅ User Accounts & Cloud Storage:
  
  🔐 Personal Research Vault – Save and access previous simulations, DNA data, environmental monitoring logs
  
  📂 Community Contributions – Share datasets, findings, and reports
 

- `2024-10-07` **nodefather**: The AI-Scientist from SakanaAI is an open-source project designed for automating the scientific process through AI models. It leverages techniques like Bayesian optimization, reinforcement learning, and evolutionary algorithms to generate hypotheses, design experiments, and analyze data autonomously. 
  
  For Mycosoft, this tool could be integrated into NatureOS for automating fungal research. For example, it could help optimize mushroom growth conditions, manage large datasets from MushroomOne or SporeBase, or automate scientific discoveries related to mycelium signal processing. The backend can be enhanced to work with the Mycorrhizae Protocol for real-time scientific insights.

- `2024-11-26` **nodefather**: 1. Review of AMG's NDA
  
  The NDA provided by AMG appears to have the following structure (from the file's details):
  
  Key Sections to Review for Risks:
  
  1. Definition of Confidential Information:
  Ensure their definition is broad but does not unfairly include information you may share in good faith (e.g., concepts you already own or public knowledge). If their clause includes vague terms like "any and all information," it might be problematic.
  
  
  2. Mutuality:
  Confirm whether the NDA is mutual or unilateral. It’s critical for your protection that the NDA explicitly states AMG will also keep your information confidential.
  
  
  3. IP Ownership:
  Some NDAs include clauses that might transfer ownership of shared ideas or work product to the receiving party. Ensure the NDA does not suggest that any insights, designs, or ideas you disclose could become AMG’s property.
  
  
  4. Duration of Obligations:
  NDAs often include a confidentiality period (e.g., 2-5 years). If

- `2026-01-15` **nodefather**: 🚨 Attention: moving forward, in regards to projects, especially new projects, new ventures, new contracts, new business opportunities and especially engineering, biz dev and contracting, I am making it a company policy to have management protocols from top down and bottom up in planning or requests be all be tied to a primary document called a SMEAC, also called a 5- Paragraph Order. If you are unfamiliar with this form of outline, I am willing and able to train all of you how it works, why its vital to my way of working will the team and the company synergistically and why its a format me, the ai and our system requires going forward. If you have any questions about this policy or feedback let me know. Thank You.
  
  The **SMEAC **5-paragraph order is a military planning format for clear, concise orders, standing for Situation, Mission, Execution, Administration & Logistics, and Command & Signal, used by US and NATO forces to organize essential mission details for small units, with t

  # Mycosoft — Monday Weekly Briefing
  
  **Week Focus:** Infrastructure, Platform Readiness, Capital & Scale
  **Objective:** Lock operational foundations (warehouse, platform, hardware) while aligning capital, insurance, and next-stage product execution.
  
  ---

  1. Dual-Use Infrastructure: Civilian + Defense
  
  Mycosoft operates at the intersection of environmental science and defense technology — building dual-use systems that serve both ecological restoration and operational intelligence needs.
  
  “Every environmental sensor we deploy doubles as a defense intelligence node.”
  
  Civil use: pollution tracking, climate data, ecological recovery.
  
  Defense use: terrain awareness, contamination mapping, operational readiness.

  We’re defining a new military and intelligence doctrine — the OEI framework — that fuses biological data, AI, and environmental sensing for situational dominance.
  
  “Environmental superiority is the new battlespace advantage.”
  
  Enhances Intelligence Preparation of the Operational Environment (IPOE).
  
  Integrates real-time terrain, air, and bio-signal data with AI-driven decision systems.
  
  Extends beyond SIGINT and M

- `2024-11-26` **nodefather** `#legal`: 1. Review of AMG's NDA
  
  The NDA provided by AMG appears to have the following structure (from the file's details):
  
  Key Sections to Review for Risks:
  
  1. Definition of Confidential Information:
  Ensure their definition is broad but does not unfairly include information you may share in good faith (e.g., concepts you already own or public knowledge). If their clause includes vague terms like "any and all information," it might be problematic.
  
  
  2. Mutuality:
  Confirm whether the NDA is mutual or unilateral. It’s critical for your protection that the NDA explicitly states AMG will also keep your information confidential.
  
  
  3. IP Ownership:
  Some NDAs include clauses that might transfer ownership of shared ideas or work product to the receiving party. Ensure the NDA

- `2025-10-11` **nodefather** `#general`: TALKING POINTS:
  
  1. Dual-Use Infrastructure: Civilian + Defense
  
  Mycosoft operates at the intersection of environmental science and defense technology — building dual-use systems that serve both ecological restoration and operational intelligence needs.
  
  “Every environmental sensor we deploy doubles as a defense intelligence node.”
  
  Civil use: pollution tracking, climate data, ecological recovery.
  
  Defense use: terrain awareness, contamination mapping, operational readiness.
  
  2. Operational Environmental Intelligence (OEI) Doctrine
  
  We’re defining a new military and intelligence doctrine — the OEI framework — that fuses biological data, AI, and environmental sensing for situational dominance.
  
  “Environmental superiority is the new battlespace advantage.”

### 💡 Ideas & Concepts

- `2024-10-06` **nodefather** `#concepts-and-ideas`: Mycosoft is pioneering earth-monitoring and biological data solutions through its NatureOS platform, leveraging field devices like Mushroom One and SporeBase for continuous environmental sensing. By utilizing soil and mycelium sensors, we offer a scalable, credible system for monitoring organic carbon in the soil, similar to MRV (Monitoring, Reporting, Verification) practices in regenerative agriculture. This enables real-time insights into soil health, carbon capture, and biodiversity restoration. Mycosoft envisions supporting global agriculture by integrating mycelium-driven carbon solutions and enhancing biodiversity through its robust data ecosystems.
  
  Our Impact:
  
  Global Ecosystem Support: Our tools aid farmers in fostering biodiversity and carbon sequestration.
  
  Sustainab

- `2024-11-15` **nodefather** `#concepts-and-ideas`: One of the first microprocessors.
  
  The Intel 4004 was developed and laid out by hand, using conventional schematics and some (at the time) quite unconventional fabricating techniques.
  
  It only had 2,600 transistors (well, I say “only,” but compared to modern CPUs with tens of billions of transistors that’s not a lot), and designing a circuit with 2,600 transistors is challenging but reasonable to do by hand.
  
  Here’s the schematic:

- `2024-10-07` **nodefather** `#natureos`: The AI-Scientist from SakanaAI is an open-source project designed for automating the scientific process through AI models. It leverages techniques like Bayesian optimization, reinforcement learning, and evolutionary algorithms to generate hypotheses, design experiments, and analyze data autonomously. 
  
  For Mycosoft, this tool could be integrated into NatureOS for automating fungal research. For example, it could help optimize mushroom growth conditions, manage large datasets from MushroomOne or SporeBase, or automate scientific discoveries related to mycelium signal processing. The backend can be enhanced to work with the Mycorrhizae Protocol for real-time scientific insights.

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather** `#natureos`: 2. NatureOS – The "Cloud Dashboard"
  
  Purpose: The heart of Mycosoft’s ecosystem—similar to Google Drive, this is where all apps, data, and devices integrate into a personalized research & nature interface.
  
  Key Components:
  
  ✅ Dashboard with Modules:
  
  📊 Live Data from Devices – Connects to personal or public Mushroom 1 & SporeBase sensors
  
  🌿 Mycology Cloud Apps – Quick access to Petri Dish Simulator, Mushroom Simulator, Compound Simulator, Ancestry Database, Spore Tracker, Map, and Identification
  
  🔗 Fungal Database API – Connect to MINDEX and submit or retrieve fungal data
  
  🛠 Device Management – Users can control Mushroom 1, SporeBase, Petraeus from their dashboard
  
  💾 Fungal Biobank Access – Request, upload, and analyze tissue samples
  
  
  ✅ User Accounts

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather** `#apps`: 3. Core Apps – "Google Apps, but for Mycology"
  
  These function like Google Docs, Sheets, and Drive, but for fungi research, simulations, and biological computing.
  
  Essential Apps:
  
  🔬 Petri Dish Simulator – A virtual growth environment for modeling mycelium interactions
  🍄 Mushroom Simulator – Simulates mushroom growth, genetic variables, and environmental impact
  🧪 Compound Simulator – Predicts fungal compound interactions, beneficial properties, and applications
  🌐 Spore Tracker – Tracks global spore movements and environmental interactions
  🗺 Fungi Map – Community-driven global mapping of fungi populations
  📜 Fungal Ancestry Database – Explore and contribute to the evolutionary history of fungi
  🤖 Myca AI Research Assistant – AI-driven assistant that overlays all apps

- `2025-01-25` **nodefather** `#mycosoft-com`: Mycosoft.com Core Product Plan
  
  Goal: Make Mycosoft.com the central hub for fungal intelligence, data, research, and tools—structured like Google’s ecosystem, with a search-first interface, cloud applications, hardware integration, and AI-assisted interaction.
  
  
  ---
  
  1. Homepage – "The Google for Fungi"
  
  Purpose: A powerful, search-driven entry point into Mycosoft’s ecosystem.
  
  Core Features:
  
  ✅ Fungal Search Engine – A search bar that connects to MINDEX, Mycorrhizae Protocol, and open datasets like MycoBank, NCBI, and iNaturalist.
  ✅ Quick Links & Shortcuts – One-click access to key areas:
  
  🌱 Buy Devices – Purchase Mushroom 1, SporeBase, TruffleBot, Petraeus
  
  🔬 Submit Tissue – Send samples to the biobank for research & sequencing
  
  🧫 Request Tissue – 
- `2025-01-25` **nodefather** `#mycosoft-com`: Monetization & Business Model
  
  To sustain and grow Mycosoft’s platform while providing free access to core tools, the business model will be tiered access, device sales, and data licensing.
  
  ✅ Free Access:
  
  Basic search, NatureOS dashboard, Myca AI, and core apps are free for general users.
  
  
  ✅ Paid Tiers & Revenue Streams:
  
  Hardware Sales – Mushroom 1, SporeBase, Petraeus, and lab tools
  
  Premium Research Subscriptions – Advanced analytics, biobank access, and data storage
  
  Enterprise Solutions – B2B licensing for biotech, agriculture, and environmental industries
  
  Cloud Processing & API Access – Paid access for large-scale research projects
  
  
  ✅ Decentralized Science Funding:
  
  MycoDAO-powered research grants, crowdfunding, and community-backed sc
- `2025-01-25` **nodefather** `#mycosoft-com`: Development Roadmap & Next Steps
  
  Phase 1 – Core Infrastructure (Q1 2025)
  
  ✅ Finalize website structure & UX
  
  ✅ Set up Mycorrhizae Protocol backend
  
  ✅ Integrate NatureOS & Myca AI
  
  ✅ Build basic device portal & network access
  
  
  Phase 2 – App Integration (Q2 2025)
  
  🔄 Fully integrate Petri Dish Simulator, Mushroom Simulator, Compound Simulator
  
  🌎 Launch Spore Tracker & Fungi Map
  
  🤖 Refine Myca AI’s NLP & voice assistant capabilities
  
  
  Phase 3 – Scaling & Community Expansion (Q3 2025+)
  
  🔬 Open-source data tools & research API
  
  🏭 Partner with biotech, agriculture, and climate science industries
  
  💰 Secure investment for full-scale expansion & decentralized research funding
- `2025-01-25` **nodefather** `#mycosoft-com`: Mycosoft.com will be the Google of fungi—a functional, interactive, and open ecosystem for understanding, interacting with, and utilizing nature. Through NatureOS, Myca AI, and a robust set of mycological tools, the platform will bridge citizen scientists, researchers, and industry professionals into a fungal knowledge network.
  
  🚀 Next Steps:
  
  Finalize homepage UI/UX wireframes
  
  Develop NatureOS MVP
  
  Build out Myca AI’s search & assistant capabilities

  A centralized hub for Mycosoft’s hardware ecosystem to enable real-world fungal computing and data collection.
  
  ✅ Buy & Set Up Devices:
  
  Mushroom 1 – Mycelium signal reader & environmental sensor
  
  SporeBase – Spore data collection & tracking device
  
  Petraeus – Petri dish biological computing interface
  
  TruffleBot – AI-driven fungal research tool
  
  
  ✅ Device Network & Data Access:
  
  📡 Connect Devices to Cloud – Users can register and manage devices via NatureOS
  
  📊 Live Dashboard for Public Data – Real-time feeds from environmental and fungal monitoring stations
  
  🧩 Open API for Researchers – Enable integrations with scientific and industrial applications

- `2025-04-17` **nodefather** `#mas-ai-system`: MCP Run Python server lets AI Agents execute Python code in a secure sandboxed environment.
  
  Uses Pyodide to run code, detects and installs dependencies, and captures all outputs - perfect for agent-driven data analysis.
  
  Works with Pydantic AI and MCP clients.

- `2025-05-05` **nodefather** `#mas-ai-system`: Fullstack Web3 Developer Roadmap
  
  1. Master Core Web Development
  
     * HTML/CSS
     * JavaScript
     * Frontend Framework (React.js)
     * Node.js & Express.js
     * Databases (SQL & NoSQL)
     * Authentication
  
  2. Learn Blockchain Basics
  
     * Blockchain Fundamentals
     * Ethereum
     * Smart Contracts (Solidity)
     * Web3.js / Ethers.js
  
  3. Master Web3 Development
  
     * Solidity (Smart Contracts)
     * Truffle/Hardhat
     * Web3 Frontend (MetaMask Integration)
     * Decentralized Storage (IPFS, Arweave)
  
  4. Learn DeFi
  
     * DeFi Concepts
     * Popular DeFi Protocols (Uniswap, Aave)
  
  5. Learn Layer-2 Solutions
  
     * Optimistic Rollups & zk-Rollups
     * Layer-2 Networks (Polygon, Arbitrum)
  
  6. Build Web3 Projects
  
     * Decentr

- `2026-01-18` **nodefather** `#mycosoft-platform`: These are some Deployment Lessons I learned as I am moving towards a more automated CI/CD Pipeline (Continuous Integration/Continuous Deployment or Delivery), which I will be implementing so all of us can modify or send to devs to modify in a clean fast way.  Also a current audit of VM which is now already changing for the better.
  
  CI/CD (Continuous Integration/Continuous Deployment or Delivery represents a set of operating principles and practices that enable software development teams to deliver code changes more frequently, reliably, and efficiently. It is a cornerstone of modern DevOps, automating the steps between developing code and deploying it to production. )

- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet** `#mycosoft-platform`: Basically.
  
  Set statics and ports so that they are a little easier to manage.
- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet** `#mycosoft-platform`: # Myca VM Network & Port Scheme
  
  - Production
  - Sandbox
  - Test
  
  The goals are:
  - Predictability
  - Minimal accidental exposure
  - Clear separation of environments
  - Easy mental mapping at 02:00 during incident response
  
  ---
  
  ## 1. VM Inventory
  
  | Environment | Hostname (example)        | Static IP     |
  |------------|---------------------------|---------------|
  | Production | myca-prod                 | x.x.x.201     |
  | Sandbox    | myca-sandbox              | x.x.x.202     |
  | Test       | myca-test                 | x.x.x.203     |
  | (Optional) Shared / Observability | myca-ops | x.x.x.204 |
  | (Optional) Bastion / VPN | myca-bastion | x.x.x.205 |
  
  All VMs run:
  - Docker
  - Supabase
  - Reverse proxy (Traefik / NPM / Caddy)
  - Linux firewa
- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet** `#mycosoft-platform`: ---
  
  ## 3. Host-Level Listening Ports
  
  ### Production (.201)
  
  | Port | Scope | Purpose |
  |-----|------|---------|
  | 80  | WAN  | HTTP → HTTPS redirect |
  | 443 | WAN  | HTTPS (reverse proxy) |
  | 8443 | LAN/VPN (optional) | Admin / debug HTTPS |
  | 22  | LAN/VPN only | SSH |
  
  ---
  
  ### Sandbox (.202)
  
  | Port | Scope | Purpose |
  |-----|------|---------|
  | 8080 | LAN/VPN only | HTTP (reverse proxy) |
  | 8443 | LAN/VPN only | HTTPS (reverse proxy) |
  | 22   | LAN/VPN only | SSH |
  
  `80/443` **closed** on sandbox to prevent mistakes.
  
  ---
  
  ### Test (.203)
  
  | Port | Scope | Purpose |
  |-----|------|---------|
  | 8081 | LAN/VPN only | HTTP (reverse proxy) |
  | 8444 | LAN/VPN only | HTTPS (reverse proxy) |
  | 22   | LAN/VPN only | SSH |
  
  
- `2026-01-23` **garretbaquet** `#mycosoft-platform`: ---
  
  ## 6. Supabase Notes (Critical)
  
  - Postgres **must not** be exposed to WAN
  - Prefer:
    - Docker-internal networking
    - Access via VPN or SSH tunnel only
  - Only expose Supabase services that clients explicitly need
  - Treat Supabase as a private backend, not a public DB
  
  ---
  
  ## 7. Firewall Rules (Summary)
  
  ### Production (.201)
  Allow:
  - WAN → 80, 443
  - LAN/VPN → SSH, admin ports
  Block:
  - Everything else
  
  ### Sandbox / Test (.202 / .203)
  Allow:
  - LAN/VPN → reverse proxy ports
  - LAN/VPN → SSH
  Block:
  - All WAN inbound traffic
  
  ---
  
  ## 8. Port Philosophy (Why This Works)
  
  - Environment separation is **network-enforced**
  - Port numbers remain predictable
  - Docker configs stay clean (standard ports internally)
  - DNS-bas
